 Decisions related to the legal, rules and tax rates related to the new tax system have been taken in the GST Council meetings

 The council was formed on 15 September 2016 as the first federal institution in the country

 Out of these, more than 96 percent decisions have already been implemented through 294 notifications issued by the Central Government
 ' shesh faisle kriyanvayan ke vibhinn staron par hai
 Notifications related to this have been issued by the same number of states
 ' The statement said that the functioning of the GST Council has started a new phase of cooperative federalism, in which the central and state governments collectively take collective decisions related to the indirect tax system

 hangal ne may main jab 'madhubala' naamak tivi sho main ek kirdaar ke liye sahmati di thi, tab unhone kaha tha, "main maanata hum ki kaam karne kii koi umr seemaa nahin hoti
 "he was still ill at the time, but was not ready to give up
 tippaniyan All Bollywood celebrities paid tribute to Hangal
 abhinetri shabana azmi ne kaha ki hangal ke nidhan ke saath ek yug kaa ant ho gaya
 Several leaders including Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) leader LK Advani and BJP President Nitin Gadkari mourned his death
 hangal kaa parthiv sharir ravivaar dopaher panchtatv main villin ho gaya
 Hangal, the son of Hangal, lit him
 vah kuulhe kii haddi tut jane ke kaaran lambe samay se biimaar the

 hangal ke bete vijay (76) ne bataaya, "mere pita kaa subah nau baje ke kareeb nidhan ho gaya
 He died mainly due to age-related reasons
 unke fefde kamjor ho gaye the or kaam karnaa band kar diya tha
 "he said," i am saddened at my father's demise
 lekin koi kya kar saktaa he, sabhi ko ek din janaa hi he
 "hangal's funeral took place at 1 am at the Vile Parle cremation ground
 hangal kaa ilaaj kar rahe chikitsak kaulsom hossain ne bataaya, "vah kuulhe kii haddi tut jane se peedit the or unke fefde or gurde ke kaam band kar dene ke kaaran unki maut ho gai
 " hangal ke santakruj sthit nivas par unke parivaar ke ek sadsy ne bataaya, "yah hamaare parivaar, unke prashansakon or puri film birdari ke liye bada jhatka or nuksaan he
 " aspataal ke adhikariyon ke anusaar hangal beeti 16 agast se kuulhe kii haddi tut jane ke kaaran aashaa paarekh aspataal main bhartee the
 He was suffering from diseases of old age for a long time
 apni patni ke nidhan ke baad se vah apane bete vijay ke saath rahete the
 Born in Sialkot (pakistan), Hangal spent most of his childhood in Peshawar
 vah ek darji ke rup main bade hue, lekin rangamanch ke jariye unhone apni pyaas bujhaai
 After partition, he moved to Mumbai in 1949
 vah vampanth se sambaddh pipuls theatre association (ipta) se jude hue the
 IPTA also once attracted Balraj Sahni, Utpal Dutt, Kaifi Azmi and many more
 hangal ne 1966-67 main hindi filmon main pravesh kiya
 His early films include 'teesri Kasam' and 'shagird'
 ek abhinayta ke rup main cinema ke saath unhone apni shuruyaat 50 kii umr main kii thi, isliye bhoomikaaon ke lihaaj se unke paas bahut vikalp nahin bache the
 But he happily and responsibly played the roles of an uncle, father and grandfather of heroes and heroines
 charitra abhinayta ke rup main unhen 'sholay' main rahim chachaa kii bhoomika ke liye yaad kiya jaataa he
 Some of his memorable films include 'namak Haram', 'sholay', 'bawarchi', 'chupa Rustom', 'abhimaan' and 'guddi' and who can forget his role in 'shaukeen', in which he has retired Played the role of an old man
 hangal kii adhikansh filmein desh ke pratham superstar rajesh khanna ke saath thim, jinka haal hi main 18 july ko nidhan ho gaya
 Hangal had worked with Rajesh Khanna in 'aapki Kasam', 'amardeep', 'phir Wahi Raat' and 'stepha Bhai'
 hangal apane putr vijay ke saath santakruj sthit ek flats main rahete the
 He also appeared in Aamir Khan's 'lagaan' (2001) and Shah Rukh Khan's 'paheli' (2006)
 hangal varsh 2011 main us samay surkhiyon main aa gaye the, jab yah baat saamne ai thi ki vah apni aay ke saadhan khatm ho jane ke baad aajeevika ke liye sangharsh kar rahe hai or unke paas bhojan or dawaaiyon tak ke liye paise nahin bache the
 After this, many people from the film industry like actors Amitabh Bachchan and Aamir Khan offered him financial help
 96 varsh kii umr main unhone wheelchair par baithkar fishan parade kii thi
 At the age of 97, he lent his voice in the animated film and appeared in the small screen serial 'madhubala'
 is tarah hangal ne antim saans tak fan ke prati apana junun marane nahin diya
 When Hangal agreed in May for a role in a TV show called 'madhubala', he said, "I agree that there is no age limit to work
" " vah us samay bhi biimaar the, lekin haar maanane ko taiyaar nahin the
 The comments bollywood se judi tamaam hastiyon ne hangal ko shradhanjali di
 Actress Shabana Azmi said that an era came to an end with Hangal's demise
 bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani or bhaajapa adhyaksh nitin gadakari sahit kai netaaon ne unke nidhan par shok jataayaa
 Hangal's son Vijay (76) said, "my father passed away around 9 am
 unki maut mukhyarup se umr sambandhit kaarnon se hui he
 His lungs had weakened and stopped working
 " unhone kaha, "main apane pitaaji ke nidhan par dukhi hum
 But what one can do, everyone has to go one day
 " hangal kaa antim sanskaar ek baje viley parley shmashaan ghat par hua
 Doctor Kaulsoom Hussain, who is treating Hangal, said, "he was suffering from a hip fracture and died due to his lung and kidney function being stopped
" " a family member at Hangal's residence in Santa Cruz said, "it is a big shock and loss for our family, their fans and the entire film fraternity
" " According to hospital officials, Hangal was admitted to Asha Parekh Hospital since August 16 due to a hip fracture
 vah lambe samay se budhaape kii bimariyon se peedit the
 He lived with his son Vijay after his wife passed away
 sialkot (pakistan) main paidaa hue hangal ne apana adhikansh bachapan peshawar main bitaayaa tha
 He grew up as a tailor, but quenched his thirst through theater
 vibhaajan ke baad vah 1949 main mumbai chale aae
 He was associated with the People's Theater Association (IPTA) affiliated to the Left
 ipta ne kabhi balraj saahani, utpal dutt, caphi azmi or kai anya ko bhi aakarshith kiya tha
 Hangal entered Hindi films in 1966–67
 unki shuruaati filmon main 'teesri kasam' or 'shagird' shaamil hai
 He made his debut with cinema as an actor at the age of 50, so he did not have many options in terms of roles
 lekin unhone khushi-khushi or puri jimmedaari ke saath nayak or nayikaon ke chachaa, pita or dada kii bhoomikaayen nibhaain
 As a character actor, he is remembered for his role as Rahim Chacha in 'sholay'
 unki kuch yaadgaar filmon main 'namak haraam', 'sholay', 'bawarchi', 'chupa rustam', 'abhimaan' or 'guddi' shaamil hai or 'shaukeen' main bhala unki bhoomika ko koun bhul saktaa he, jisamen unhone ek sevanivrutt buudhe vyakti kii bhoomika nibhaai thi
 Most of Hangal's films were with the country's first superstar Rajesh Khanna, who recently died on 18 July
 hangal ne rajesh khanna ke saath 'aapaki kasam', 'amardip', 'phir vahi raat' or 'sautela bhai' main kaam kiya tha
 Hangal lived with his son Vijay in a flat in Santa Cruz
 vah aamir khan kii 'lagaan' (2001) or shahrukh khan kii 'paheli' (2006) main bhi dikhe the
 Hangal made headlines in 2011 when it was revealed that he was struggling for a livelihood after his income was exhausted and he had no money left for food and medicines
 iske baad abhinayta amitabh bachchan or aamir khan jaise film udyog ke bahut se logon ne unhen aarthik madad kii peshkash kii thi
 At the age of 96, she did a fashion parade in a wheelchair

 ek abhinayta ke rup main cinema ke saath unhone apni shuruyaat 50 kii umr main kii thi, isliye bhoomikaaon ke lihaaj se unke paas bahut vikalp nahin bache the
 But he happily and responsibly played the roles of an uncle, father and grandfather of heroes and heroines
 charitra abhinayta ke rup main unhen 'sholay' main rahim chachaa kii bhoomika ke liye yaad kiya jaataa he
 Some of his memorable films include 'namak Haram', 'sholay', 'bawarchi', 'chupa Rustom', 'abhimaan' and 'guddi' and who can forget his role in 'shaukeen', in which he has retired Played the role of an old man
 hangal kii adhikansh filmein desh ke pratham superstar rajesh khanna ke saath thim, jinka haal hi main 18 july ko nidhan ho gaya
 Hangal had worked with Rajesh Khanna in 'aapki Kasam', 'amardeep', 'phir Wahi Raat' and 'stepha Bhai'
 hangal apane putr vijay ke saath santakruj sthit ek flats main rahete the
 He also appeared in Aamir Khan's 'lagaan' (2001) and Shah Rukh Khan's 'paheli' (2006)
 hangal varsh 2011 main us samay surkhiyon main aa gaye the, jab yah baat saamne ai thi ki vah apni aay ke saadhan khatm ho jane ke baad aajeevika ke liye sangharsh kar rahe hai or unke paas bhojan or dawaaiyon tak ke liye paise nahin bache the
 After this, many people from the film industry like actors Amitabh Bachchan and Aamir Khan offered him financial help
 96 varsh kii umr main unhone wheelchair par baithkar fishan parade kii thi
 At the age of 97, he lent his voice in the animated film and appeared in the small screen serial 'madhubala'
 is tarah hangal ne antim saans tak fan ke prati apana junun marane nahin diya

" " vah us samay bhi biimaar the, lekin haar maanane ko taiyaar nahin the

 bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani or bhaajapa adhyaksh nitin gadakari sahit kai netaaon ne unke nidhan par shok jataayaa
 As a character actor, he is remembered for his role as Rahim Chacha in 'sholay'
